<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great location, couple items to be aware of We stayed at the Hotel Plaza Mayor April 13-16, 2005, and it truly is a good bargain within walking distance of many of Madrid's major sites. However, as with most things in life, you get what you pay for. When we checked in, it was apparent that the bed linens had not been cleaned as there was something that looked suspiciously like dried blood on the sheets. I had to take them out to the cleaning staff and ask for replacements. Second, the heating unit in our room did not work until our 3rd night, which made for 2 cold nights (the weather in Madrid dropped to 8 degrees Celsius at night), despite asking the staff for help. Third, the room sizes are good only by European standards (or for any place where space is at a premium, like New York) - they are not spacious by any means, and they are downright tiny by comparison with most hotels throughout America. I am a Medium person in the U.S., but I literally had to squeeze into the shower. Overall, though, it probably is a great place if you don't plan to spend much time in your hotel room or if the weather outside is comfortable.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Friendliest hotel staff in Spain! We spent two nights in this excellent hotel. The location can't be beat for proximity to the lively Plaza Mayor, the rooms are clean and excellent for the price. Not fancy schmancy, just nice. Most people don't spend their time in Madrid in the hotel room anyway. So much to see and this location is within easy walking distance to the Royal Palace, Prado, the Caves, shops, cafes and restaurants galore.We found the front desk staff to be the most hospitable in Spain during our three weeks of travel! Extremely friendly - bright and cheery in the morning, afternoon and night. I don't know where they found the people at the front desk or the rest of the hotel staff we saw but these were by far the most welcoming people in the hospitality industry that we experienced in our 3 weeks of traveling throughout Spain. It is so nice to be greeted by a friendly desk clerk when you are checking into a hotel after traveling (or shopping!) all day. Our son spent most of one day in bed with a sore throat and cough- the front desk expressed concern about him and commented to him that they were glad he was feeling better when he was ready to get up and go again. Unrequested by us, housekeeping went up late in the afternoon to make up our room since they hadn't been able to get in to it while he was sleeping. Just a nice little thing but it's the little things that matter to you when you are traveling and away from home.  Hotel Plaza Mayor and its accomodating staff are rare find anywhere and certainly standout in the big, bustling city of Madrid.

<Author>aussiekaye
<Content>best hotel location in madrid We stayed at the hotel Plaza Mayor over the easter weekend. I decided to book it after reading the reviews here and I couldn't have been happier with the hotel. We stayed in a triple room which was a little cramped but we did have a lot of luggage with us. The room was very clean although nothing fancy. The only complaint I had was that the sheets on the beds were not big enough and after a night sleep we all woke up to find ourselves sleeping on the mattress but after mentioning our problem to the front desk the problem was fixed by using double bed sheets. The hotel staff couldn't have been more friendly and helpful. The location of the hotel cannot be beaten. We walked everywhere and found it so nice to be able to just walk to the plaza mayor in the evening for an hour or so. For 80 euros a night you will not find better in Madrid.

<Author>OD
<Content>great place Date: March 7, 8  10We had a lovely time at the Hotel Plaza Mayor. We stayed in room 503, a wonderful room at the front of the building on the 5th floor. A big room (for Madrid standards) with two big windows that opened and we could look out on the little square (Plaza Santa Cruz, I think it was?) to see everything going on. While there was no airconditioning, the room cooled off very nicely with just opening the windows.This hotel is not on Plaza Mayor actually but 1 block away, which meant that things quieted down quite nicely after 11 p.m., and also being up high meant we had less street noise. It is a small intimate hotel, and we really liked that.The staff could not have been more helpful with directions, suggestions for dinner, and help with the luggage. We actually left some luggage at the hotel when we went to Toledo one day. We stayed overnight in Toledo. When we came back to the hotel, they had us in the same room that we liked and our luggage all ready.The only reason I did not give this a 5 spot ranking is that we would have liked to have a drink when we got back after sightseeing, and relax a bit. But their little bar was closed, and the foyer of the hotel was underconstruction. The breakfast room was pleasant, and the breakfast while adequate was too expensive for what we got. We learned to have breakfast at a little cafeteria just around the corner. The carpet of our room was never vacuumed which I though odd and mentioned it at the front desk. They said they had plans to replace it. But everything was great apart from that. We felt very safe there day and night. This was helped by the fact that there was a big police presence in the square at all hours. We found out when we watched TV that an International Conference on Terrorism was being held in Madrid and one of the venues was a conference building about 300 ft. away on our little square! Political leaders from all over the world were attending! Then we understood why there were so many police directing traffic, standing around, and moving cars on the little square!We took the metro at Puerta del Sol and went everywhere. It was so easy to use. We loved the Prado - spent all day there and didn't see it all. We could have spent a second day at the Prado, but went to the Reina Sofia which was also wonderful.  
<Date>Apr 3, 2005

<Author>drg0nz0
<Content>Top Notch I stayed at Plaza Mayor for four nights with my girlfriend and we had a wonderful time. The hotel could not be any more perfectly placed for touring the city. It is a very short walk from the Sol Metro station (which is the heart of Madrid's metro system) and even closer to Plaza Mayor and the Old City. The rooms are clean and spacious, the hotel is clean and modern, and the staff is very accomodating. I needed to get the train schedule for the RENFE to Barcelona but the customer service people at RENFE spoke very fast (my spainish is only so-so) and I couldn't understand them. One of the fellows at the front desk called them for me and got the schedule. The area is safe and well lit. As with any city on the planet: the only unsafe streets are the streets you're on by yourself. When I go back to Madrid, I'll be staying at Hotel Plaza Mayor again. This hotel easily competes with the 4-star folks that offer laundry service and health clubs.

<Author>PlasticWelshman
<Content>No public transport required.... Stayed at this hotel with a group of friends in February 2005. The first thing you notice about this hotel is the superb location (just off the Plaza Mayor which is one of the main squares in Madrid) - we didn't use any public transport all weekend as everything was in easy walking distance. The next and possibly most important feature is the cleanliness of this hotel - it easily rivals standards set by much more expensive hotels. To top it all, the staff were all very helpful and friendly - even when we were slightly drunk!!! Madrid is a fantastic city but this hotel definitely made the weekend extra special. I have since recommended it to friends who are visiting Madrid this year and have no doubts that I will stay here again. A top class hotel with very reasonable rates.
